Implements \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a4c9310943a436bd6b39e9d0e98a9bc9e}{org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}.

\hypertarget{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a9b4a2c53e26a3643b45e824d40dd142b}{\index{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}!contains\-Annotation\-Property\-In\-Signature@{contains\-Annotation\-Property\-In\-Signature}}
\index{contains\-Annotation\-Property\-In\-Signature@{contains\-Annotation\-Property\-In\-Signature}!uk::ac::manchester::cs::owl::owlapi::OWLOntologyImpl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}}
\subsubsection[{contains\-Annotation\-Property\-In\-Signature}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}boolean uk.\-ac.\-manchester.\-cs.\-owl.\-owlapi.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl.\-contains\-Annotation\-Property\-In\-Signature (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf I\-R\-I}}]{owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I, }
\item[{boolean}]{include\-Imports\-Closure}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a9b4a2c53e26a3643b45e824d40dd142b}
Determines if the signature of this ontology, or possibly the signature of one of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology, contains an O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property that has the specified I\-R\-I. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} & The I\-R\-I of the O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property to check for \\
\hline
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & {\ttfamily true} if the signature of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology should be checked, {\ttfamily false} if just the signature of this ontology should be chekced. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=true} then returns {\ttfamily true} if there is an O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property with {\ttfamily owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I in the signature of at least one ontology in the imports clousre of this ontology and {\ttfamily false} if this is not the case. If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=false} then returns {\ttfamily true} if the signature of this ontology contains an O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property that has {\ttfamily owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I and {\ttfamily false} if the signature of this ontology does not contain a class with {\ttfamily owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_ad7ccfc047d448a306e698f867a33328a}
Determines if this ontology contains the specified axiom, but ignoring any annotations on this axiom. For example, if the ontology contains {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(Annotation(p V) A B)} then this method will return {\ttfamily true} if the ontology contains {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(\-A B)} or {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(Annotation(q S) A B)} for any annotation property {\ttfamily q} and any annotation value {\ttfamily S}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em axiom} & The axiom to test for. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if this ontology contains this axiom with or without annotations. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Determines if this ontology and possibly its imports closure contains the specified axiom but ignoring any annotations on this axiom. For example, if the ontology contains {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(Annotation(p V) A B)} then this method will return {\ttfamily true} if the ontology contains {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(\-A B)} or {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(Annotation(q S) A B)} for any annotation property {\ttfamily q} and any annotation value {\ttfamily S}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em axiom} & The axiom to test for. \\
\hline
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & if {\ttfamily true} the imports closure of this ontology will be searched for the specified axiom. If {\ttfamily false} only this ontology will be searched for the specifed axiom. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if this ontology contains this axiom with or without annotations. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{contains\-Data\-Property\-In\-Signature@{contains\-Data\-Property\-In\-Signature}!uk::ac::manchester::cs::owl::owlapi::OWLOntologyImpl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}}
\subsubsection[{contains\-Data\-Property\-In\-Signature}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}boolean uk.\-ac.\-manchester.\-cs.\-owl.\-owlapi.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl.\-contains\-Data\-Property\-In\-Signature (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a2496c634bf8c722f098c4ccdb85a25a6}
Determines if the signature of this ontology, or possibly the signature of one of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology, contains an O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property that has the specified I\-R\-I. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owl\-Data\-Property\-I\-R\-I} & The I\-R\-I of the O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property to check for \\
\hline
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & {\ttfamily true} if the signature of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology should be checked, {\ttfamily false} if just the signature of this ontology should be chekced. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=true} then returns {\ttfamily true} if there is an O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property with {\ttfamily owl\-Data\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I in the signature of at least one ontology in the imports clousre of this ontology and {\ttfamily false} if this is not the case. If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=false} then returns {\ttfamily true} if the signature of this ontology contains an O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property that has {\ttfamily owl\-Data\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I and {\ttfamily false} if the signature of this ontology does not contain a class with {\ttfamily owl\-Data\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em owl\-Entity} & The entity \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if the ontology contains a reference to the specified entity, otherwise {\ttfamily false} The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & {\ttfamily true} if the signature of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology should be checked, {\ttfamily false} if just the signature of this ontology should be chekced. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=true} then returns {\ttfamily true} if there is an O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property with {\ttfamily owl\-Object\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I in the signature of at least one ontology in the imports clousre of this ontology and {\ttfamily false} if this is not the case. If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=false} then returns {\ttfamily true} if the signature of this ontology contains an O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property that has {\ttfamily owl\-Object\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I and {\ttfamily false} if the signature of this ontology does not contain a class with {\ttfamily owl\-Object\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its I\-R\-I. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{get\-Axioms@{get\-Axioms}!uk::ac::manchester::cs::owl::owlapi::OWLOntologyImpl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Axioms}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Axiom}$>$ uk.\-ac.\-manchester.\-cs.\-owl.\-owlapi.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl.\-get\-Axioms (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a0244a8caaf5beb560fe0c9b93cceb956}
Retrieves all of the axioms in this ontology. Note that to test whether or not this ontology is empty (i.\-e. contains no axioms, the is\-Empty method is preferred over \hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a0244a8caaf5beb560fe0c9b93cceb956}{get\-Axioms()}.\hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a7016e951aee89c95705e175b6ea1fa9c}{is\-Empty()}. )

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set of all axioms in this ontology, including logical axioms and annotation axioms. The set that is returned is a copy of the axioms in the ontology -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is recommended that the {\ttfamily contains\-Axiom} method is used to determine whether or not this ontology contains a particular axiom rather than using \hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a0244a8caaf5beb560fe0c9b93cceb956}{get\-Axioms()}.contains(). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item[{boolean}]{include\-Imports\-Closure}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Gets the classes that are in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the imports closure of this ontology.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether classes should be drawn from the signature of just this ontology or the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily true} then the set of classes returned will correspond to the union of the classes in the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily false} then the set of classes returned will correspond to the classes that are in the signature of this just this ontology. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of classes that are in the signature of this ontology and possibly the union of the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the datatypes that are in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the imports closure of this ontology. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_acf4f6dc1a65552a6bdcc4402a1efd221}{get\-Signature()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether datatypes should be drawn from the signature of just this ontology or the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily true} then the set of datatypes returned will correspond to the union of the datatypes in the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily false} then the set of datatypes returned will correspond to the datatypes that are in the signature of this just this ontology. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of datatypes that are in the signature of this ontology and possibly the union of the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{get\-Direct\-Imports@{get\-Direct\-Imports}!uk::ac::manchester::cs::owl::owlapi::OWLOntologyImpl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Gets the set of {\itshape loaded} ontologies that this ontology is related to via the directly\-Imports relation. See Section 3.\-4 of the O\-W\-L 2 specification for the definition of the directly\-Imports relation. 

Note that there may be fewer ontologies in the set returned by this method than there are I\-R\-Is in the set returned by the \hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a4f047c5e8d5b7fa3a18039c166b0106e}{get\-Direct\-Imports\-Documents()} method. This will be the case if some of the ontologies that are directly imported by this ontology are not loaded for what ever reason. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of ontologies such that for this ontology O, and each ontology O' in the set, (O, O') is in the directly\-Imports relation.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception} & If this ontology is no longer managed by its manager because it was removed from the manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

Gets the set of disjoint union axioms that have the specified class as the named class that is equivalent to the disjoint union of operands. For example, if the ontology contained the axiom Disjoint\-Union(A, prop\-P some C, D, E) this axiom would be returned for class A (but not for D or E).

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the entities in the signature of this ontology that have the specified I\-R\-I.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em iri} & The I\-R\-I of the entities to be retrieved. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of entities that are in the signature of this ontology that have the specified I\-R\-I. The set will be empty if there are no entities in the signature of this ontology with the specified I\-R\-I. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item[{{\bf I\-R\-I}}]{iri, }
\item[{boolean}]{include\-Imports\-Closure}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_adadeeab85688b8889cee8b1f28836aa0}
Gets the entities in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the signature of the imports closure of this ontology, that have the specified I\-R\-I.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em iri} & The I\-R\-I of the entitied to be retrieved. \\
\hline
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies if the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology should also be taken into account \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=true} then returns a set of entities that are in the signature of this ontology or the signature of an ontology in the imports closure of this ontology that have {\ttfamily iri} as their I\-R\-I. If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=false} then returns the entities in the signature of just this ontology that have {\ttfamily iri} as their I\-R\-I. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets all of the equivalent axioms in this ontology that contain the specified class as an operand.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cls} & The class \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_ac8c41f07e12fc42476c0bbba91a59c4d}
Gets the set of general axioms in this ontology. This includes\-: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Subclass axioms that have a complex class as the subclass 
\item Equivalent class axioms that don't contain any named classes ({\ttfamily O\-W\-L\-Class}es) 
\item Disjoint class axioms that don't contain any named classes ({\ttfamily O\-W\-L\-Class}es) 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set that is returned is a copy of the axioms in the ontology -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Implements \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_aab8e452dd05664d63c4bcf9cea86cbb5}{org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}.

\hypertarget{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a4e1e3fce87307560a544be82cf98ed86}{\index{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}!get\-Imports@{get\-Imports}}
\index{get\-Imports@{get\-Imports}!uk::ac::manchester::cs::owl::owlapi::OWLOntologyImpl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Imports}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Ontology}$>$ uk.\-ac.\-manchester.\-cs.\-owl.\-owlapi.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl.\-get\-Imports (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) throws {\bf Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception}}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a4e1e3fce87307560a544be82cf98ed86}
Gets the set of {\itshape loaded} ontologies that this ontology is related to via the {\itshape transitive closure} of the \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#Imports}{\tt directly\-Imports relation}. 

For example, if this ontology imports ontology B, and ontology B imports ontology C, then this method will return the set consisting of ontology B and ontology C. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set of ontologies that this ontology is related to via the transitive closure of the directly\-Imports relation. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception} & if this ontology is no longer managed by its manager because it was removed from the manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\hypertarget{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a0a431d2a07b584d9d868408ed5a4daf4}{\index{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}!get\-Imports\-Closure@{get\-Imports\-Closure}}
\index{get\-Imports\-Closure@{get\-Imports\-Closure}!uk::ac::manchester::cs::owl::owlapi::OWLOntologyImpl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Imports\-Closure}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Ontology}$>$ uk.\-ac.\-manchester.\-cs.\-owl.\-owlapi.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl.\-get\-Imports\-Closure (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) throws {\bf Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception}}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a0a431d2a07b584d9d868408ed5a4daf4}
Gets the set of {\itshape loaded} ontologies that this ontology is related to via the {\itshape reflexive transitive closure} of the directly\-Imports relation as defined in Section 3.\-4 of the O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification. (i.\-e. The set returned includes all ontologies returned by the \hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_a4e1e3fce87307560a544be82cf98ed86}{get\-Imports()} method plus this ontology.)

For example, if this ontology imports ontology B, and ontology B imports ontology C, then this method will return the set consisting of this ontology, ontology B and ontology C. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set of ontologies in the reflexive transitive closure of the directly\-Imports relation.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception} & If this ontology is no longer managed by its manager because it was removed from the manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}


Implements \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a0498eba3a4ae9f428b85a629e0263a8f}{org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}.

\hypertarget{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_afbfd2b7a17893f68058c9a31859a1d3f}{\index{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl@{uk\-::ac\-::manchester\-::cs\-::owl\-::owlapi\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Impl}!get\-Imports\-Declarations@{get\-Imports\-Declarations}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_afbfd2b7a17893f68058c9a31859a1d3f}
Gets the set of imports declarations for this ontology. The set returned represents the set of I\-R\-Is that correspond to the set of I\-R\-Is in an ontology's directly\-Imports\-Documents (see Section 3 in the O\-W\-L 2 structural specification).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set of imports declarations that correspond to the set of ontology document I\-R\-Is that are directly imported by this ontology. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item[{boolean}]{include\-Imports\-Closure}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_ab828c30c260e4e668cf1b7371ba89c77}
Gets the individuals that are in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the imports closure of this ontology. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_acf4f6dc1a65552a6bdcc4402a1efd221}{get\-Signature()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether individuals should be drawn from the signature of just this ontology or the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily true} then the set of individuals returned will correspond to the union of the individuals in the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily false} then the set of individuals returned will correspond to the individuals that are in the signature of this just this ontology. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of individuals that are in the signature of this ontology and possibly the union of the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_impl_ae1b51a511e84c176b6fdf9004fdf986a}
Gets the object properties that are in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the imports closure of this ontology.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether object properties should be drawn from the signature of just this ontology or the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily true} then the set of object properties returned will correspond to the union of the object properties in the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily false} then the set of object properties returned will correspond to the object properties that are in the signature of this just this ontology. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of object properties that are in the signature of this ontology and possibly the union of the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the entities that are in the signature of this ontology. The signature of an ontology is the set of entities that are used to build axioms and annotations in the ontology. (See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#Entities.2C_Literals.2C_and_Anonymous_Individuals}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification})


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether or not the returned set of entities should represent the signature of just this ontology, or the signature of the imports closure of this ontology. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of {\ttfamily O\-W\-L\-Entity} objects. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
